Nicest coin laundry place I have ever visited! Clean, well kept, a great variety of detergents/dryer sheets/drinks/snacks/etc.. available in the vending machine. Coin machine on site. They also have an app so you can pay via your phone w QR codes on the machines- how high tech and cool is that! < Text>
I live down the street from this subway, naturally when I'm hungry this is a first choice for me. There have been several times that I have been dissatisfied with the way this place has been run and I've thought about leaving this review before. I wouldn't do this sort of thing normally, but today pushed me over the edge.

I waited for a total of 30 minutes today behind one customer. This customer ordered more than 8 sandwiches and there was only one person on staff at the time. The other came back from lunch early to help with the amount of backup that had been occurring. Every time I come here and its like this I don't get angry at the people working behind the counter because they are doing the best they can, and they are working fast to get what needs to be done done.

I wholeheartedly believe that there is a huge management problem and a huge disconnect with the people that run this place with how the operations actually work. I'm only writing this review because I'm hoping that someone in management at this restaurant might actually change the way things are working and think about the experience they are creating for their employees, which then extends to your customer. I hope you fix this, for now I'll travel the extra mile to the next subway on Sante Fe.<//Text>

Highly recommend love this place. The exterior is clean and well kept, but easy to miss (No Open Sign in the huge window that faces Capital mall). Placed just about midway between the tower bridge and the Capital building. Great food served hot with good service. Nice menu selection to fill you up or just tie you over. <review>I don't generally write reviews, but I had to share my experience at Old Soul on Capitol Mall from this morning. <userid>110107883099937519995</userid>< user_name>
Lisa Shelton<//user_name>
<Time>1500156439636< /Time>< Rate>
5<//Rate>
< Review>
We had a work get together with a large group on a Friday night and there were no issues with services. Smooth as silk.
The meats are tender and the spices are fantastic! My favorite meat is the spicy pork!! (Warning: It has a kick if you aren't used to spicy foods!)
The dipping sauces have great flavor as do the "non-spicy" meats.
The experience of cooking your food at your table is great! If you have questions on how to do it, the staff is wonderful about showing you. Just ask! It's a family owned business so their heart and soul are in everything.
Be sure to enter off of Lancaster Blvd., otherwise it's tricky to find from inside the Marketplace.< /Review>

< Text>
This place is great. It's run by a Korean couple and they know their stuff. You cook your food on a grill in your table, which just adds to the meal. The buffet options are all very good, and they even have hotdogs for the picky eaters. The banchan is also excellent. I personally love the broccoli - I could eat a while plate of that!  If you are looking for some authentic Korean BBQ, then this is the place to go.</Text>

105810894131954799398< /userid>
<user_name>BuBoNiC NATE<//user_name>< date>
1471769358152<//date>
< rate>
5<//rate>
< review>
In short - good food, place looks great; good place to take a date.

My wife and I had dinner here to celebrate her promotion at work and had a great time.  First, just walking in - the lobby looks amazing.  The whole place has fairly high ceilings which gives it an open feel.  It also lets the noises dissipate quicker, so even though there were other people dining in the restaurant, we couldn't hear them as loudly as we would if the ceilings had been lower. We liked how clean the place was and the decor. We got the "All You Can Eat"  "Course #1".  With drinks our total was around 47 dollars for the two of us.  They have New Castle, Pacifico, Blue Moon and Coors on tap.  Like most Korean BBQ places they bring out plates of meat for you to cook on the grill in the center of the table.  Our waiter (like every staff member we ran into) was very polite, kind and attentive.

We enjoyed the "rib eye" which was the fairly typical thinly cut beef with seasonings that you find at Korean BBQ places and also  the spicy pork the most.  We also tried the short ribs, brisket, steak, pork belly and teriyaki chicken all of which were terrific, but were a bit more plain compared to the two dishes we enjoyed the most.

They also offer 6 sides with the meal.  We got the salad, rice, broccoli, macaroni salad, bean sprouts and kimchi.  The salad was mostly just different types of lettuce with a sweet sesame-type dressing.  It was fresh and fine for a starter.  The rice was appropriately sticky, which is preferable when eating with chopsticks.  My wife liked the kimchi, though it was a bit more spicy then she expected.

We had a great night, and will definitely be back soon!< /review>

< review>
I liked the taste of the burgers simple but not bland. It's a cozy little hole in the wall so I liked the fact that there wasn't many people for the lunch rush. They serve bottled beer as well so you can even drink if you wanted one with your burger. I got the avacado burger and added bacon it was a little pricey because you have to pay for fries and soda separate but the serving size was worth it, and the ingredients looked and tasted fresh. It's a nice place to go eat if you want a peaceful lunch and going for a nice quiet lunch date without all the distractions of a more popular spot. I'd go again if I'm ever in the area.<//review>

<Text>From the moment you take your first bite, you find out that this is not your typical burger. The bun is not your ordinary sesame bun. It is a bun with a slight pleasant crisp. If you are familiar with a Mexican Bolillo, that is what it taste and feels like.

The patties are juicy and flavorful. I specifically got the avocado burger. I enjoyed the combination of flavors it had. I wish I would have eaten it with Jalape√±os.

My wife got the Bacon Burger. The bacon was crispy and thick.

Unlike other burger joints, this place has alcoholic beverages.

I also had the Pineapple Shack. I really like it  because it was not too sweet. In fact it was the right amount of sweet.

With respect to the place appearance, It almost feels like you are going back in time to the 90s because of the decor and menu.</Text><Rating>5< /Rating>< userid>

<Rating>5</Rating>< review>
Family owned and a long time envolved in the local community. Thier burgers are amazing....the bread alone is worth the trip there. They offer a variety of amazing sides like fried zucchini, fried mushrooms etc. They do offer vegetarian options but the owner has been making my father in law sauteed mushroom sandwiches for years before a "veggie" burger was even probably thought about. Thats what keeps us going....my father in law had very few options to eat when he worked in the area 30 years ago....the owner of burger juction made him sauteed mushroom sandwiches to meet his medical need to only eat a vegetarian diet. We only go in every few months and he still recognizes  my father in law every time we go and that is so special and a tribute to how much they care. Its not a new flashy burger joint, its full of old photos and i think an old car club comes in on the weekends, but irs worth the visit. They really care about thier customer!< /review>

My burger was one of the worst burgers I've had in a long time. I called in my order today. I ordered the bacon cheeseburger. Online it said there would be 5 pieces of bacon. There was only one piece of bacon. Not even close to half of the burger had bacon on it. Might as well have had no bacon. On top of that the meat was gristly; I bit down on something hard that I had to remove from my mouth. So it made me wonder about he quality of the meat. Not much tomato on the burger either, and I love tomato. There are sooo many good burger places nowadays, I can think of like 10 off the top of my head, so therefore I would not return here. I don't know about their other burgers, but I don't reccomed the bacon cheeseburger, unless you specify that you want a lot of bacon. To me it's just unacceptable to serve me this burger with one piece of bacon. I don't know what they were thinking. And of course I had to pay extra for that measley piece of bacon. Maybe they will see this review and improve the bacon cheeseburger. But I will not give business to a place that is stingy with their ingredients. I can't stand that. Don't be cheap to save money, this seems like one of those places. Sorry if that's harsh but I'm really disappointed with this burger and I prefer to spend my money at a place that cares more about the quality of the food. I'm also disappointed that other people seemed to have good experiences and I had such a bad one. But this is definitely one of those experiences where you end up feeling like you just wasted your money cause the food was so bad. Not gonna take this risk and waste my money here again when there's so many places that always serve me a good burger.<//Review>
